   Expected backend endpoints:

const $ = (id) => document.getElementById(id);

  resolution: { mode: "single" },

const state = {
  // singles
  aiModel: "", cameraBody: "", aspectRatio: "", resolution: "",
  purpose: "", format: "", medium: "", lens: "", focalLength: "",
  shotSize: "", aperture: "", angle: "", composition: "", quality: "",
  mjVersion: "", mjStyle: "", fluxModel: "", dalleStyle: "", dalleQuality: "",
  referenceType: "", photoStyle: "", cinemaStyle: "", directorStyle: "",
  artStyle: "", colorPalette: "", mood: "", quickStyle: "", fashionFoodStyle: "",
  emotion: "", cinematicPreset: "",

  // PA groups
  lightType: { primary: "", accent: "" },
  timeOfDay: { primary: "", accent: "" },

  // multi
  lightFX: [], skinDetail: [], hairDetail: [], material: [], typography: [],

  // text/flags
  mainSubject: "", textContent: "", negativePrompt: "",
  generateFourMode: false, grid3x3Mode: false, maxConsistency: false,
  beforeAfter: false, seamlessPattern: false, skinRenderBoost: false, hairRenderBoost: false,
  seed: "", promptFormat: "flat",

  // references
  referenceWeight: 50
};

let referenceFiles = []; // File[]
let lastRequestId = 0;
let debounceTimer = null;

function notify(msg, type="info") {
  const n = $("notification");
  if (!n) return;
  n.textContent = msg;
  n.className = "notification " + (type || "info");
  n.style.display = "block";
  clearTimeout(n._t);
  n._t = setTimeout(() => { n.style.display = "none"; }, 2200);
}

function wordCount(t) {
  const s = (t || "").trim();
  return s ? s.split(/\s+/).length : 0;
}

function countParams(obj) {
  let c = 0;
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(obj || {})) {
    if (v === null || v === undefined) continue;
    if (typeof v === "string") { if (v.trim()) c++; continue; }
    if (typeof v === "boolean") { if (v) c++; continue; }
    if (Array.isArray(v)) { if (v.length) c++; continue; }
    if (typeof v === "object") {
      const inner = Object.values(v).some(x => (typeof x === "string" ? x.trim() : !!x));
      if (inner) c++;
      continue;
    }
  }
  return c;
}

/* UI selection handling */
function setSingle(group, value) {
  state[group] = value;
  document.querySelectorAll(`[data-group="${group}"]`).forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle("active", b.dataset.value === value);
    b.querySelectorAll(".slot-tag").forEach(t => t.remove());
  });
}

function toggleMulti(group, value) {
  if (!Array.isArray(state[group])) state[group] = [];
  const arr = state[group];
  const idx = arr.indexOf(value);
  if (idx >= 0) arr.splice(idx, 1);
  else arr.push(value);
  document.querySelectorAll(`[data-group="${group}"]`).forEach(b => {
    b.classList.toggle("active", arr.includes(b.dataset.value));
  });
}

function togglePrimaryAccent(group, value) {
  const cur = state[group] || { primary: "", accent: "" };
  if (cur.primary === value) cur.primary = "";
  else if (cur.accent === value) cur.accent = "";
  else if (!cur.primary) cur.primary = value;
  else if (!cur.accent) cur.accent = value;
  else cur.accent = value;
  state[group] = cur;
  syncPrimaryAccentUI(group);
}

function syncPrimaryAccentUI(group) {
  const cur = state[group] || { primary: "", accent: "" };
  document.querySelectorAll(`[data-group="${group}"]`).forEach(b => {
    const v = b.dataset.value;
    b.classList.toggle("active", v === cur.primary || v === cur.accent);
    b.querySelectorAll(".slot-tag").forEach(t => t.remove());
    if (v === cur.primary) {
      const t = document.createElement("span");
      t.className = "slot-tag primary"; t.textContent = "P";
      b.appendChild(t);
    }
    if (v === cur.accent) {
      const t = document.createElement("span");
      t.className = "slot-tag accent"; t.textContent = "A";
      b.appendChild(t);
    }
  });
}

function handleOptionClick(e) {
  const btn = e.target.closest(".option-btn");
  if (!btn || btn.disabled) return;
  const group = btn.dataset.group;
  const value = btn.dataset.value || "";
  const mode = (groupConfig[group] && groupConfig[group].mode) || "single";

  // promptFormat is a special pseudo-group (buttons still use data-group="promptFormat" in markup)
  if (group === "promptFormat") {
    state.promptFormat = value || "flat";
    document.querySelectorAll(`[data-group="promptFormat"]`).forEach(b => b.classList.toggle("active", b.dataset.value === state.promptFormat));
    scheduleGenerate();
    return;
  }

  if (mode === "single") setSingle(group, value);
  else if (mode === "multi") toggleMulti(group, value);
  else if (mode === "primaryAccent") togglePrimaryAccent(group, value);

  scheduleGenerate();
}

function syncTextAndFlags() {
  if ($("mainSubject")) state.mainSubject = $("mainSubject").value || "";
  if ($("textContent")) state.textContent = $("textContent").value || "";
  if ($("negativePrompt")) state.negativePrompt = $("negativePrompt").value || "";

  state.generateFourMode = !!($("generateFourMode") && $("generateFourMode").checked);
  state.grid3x3Mode = !!($("grid3x3Mode") && $("grid3x3Mode").checked);
  state.maxConsistency = !!($("maxConsistency") && $("maxConsistency").checked);
  state.beforeAfter = !!($("beforeAfter") && $("beforeAfter").checked);
  state.seamlessPattern = !!($("seamlessPattern") && $("seamlessPattern").checked);
  state.skinRenderBoost = !!($("skinRenderBoost") && $("skinRenderBoost").checked);
  state.hairRenderBoost = !!($("hairRenderBoost") && $("hairRenderBoost").checked);
  state.seed = ($("seedInput") && $("seedInput").value) ? $("seedInput").value : "";

  if ($("referenceWeightSlider")) {
    const v = parseInt($("referenceWeightSlider").value || "50", 10);
    state.referenceWeight = isFinite(v) ? v : 50;
  }
}

function handleImageUpload(e) {
  const files = Array.from(e.target.files || []);
  referenceFiles = files.slice(0, 13);
  // Minimal preview (names only) to avoid client-side EXIF parsing/mapping.
  const container = $("imagePreviewContainer");
  const grid = $("imagePreview");
  if (container && grid) {
    grid.innerHTML = "";
    referenceFiles.forEach(f => {
      const d = document.createElement("div");
      d.className = "image-preview-item";
      d.textContent = f.name;
      grid.appendChild(d);
    });
    container.style.display = referenceFiles.length ? "block" : "none";
  }
  scheduleGenerate();
}

function scheduleGenerate() {
  clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => { generateFromServer(); }, 280);
}

async function generateFromServer() {
  syncTextAndFlags();
  const reqId = ++lastRequestId;

  const outBox = $("promptOutput");
  const jsonBox = $("jsonOutput");
  if (outBox) outBox.textContent = "Generating‚Ä¶";
  if (jsonBox) jsonBox.textContent = "{\n  \"status\": \"generating\"\n}";

  try {
    let res;

    if (referenceFiles.length) {
      const fd = new FormData();
      fd.append("state", JSON.stringify(state));
      referenceFiles.forEach((f, i) => fd.append("images", f, f.name));
      res = await fetch("/api/prompt", { method: "POST", body: fd });
    } else {
      res = await fetch("/api/prompt", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ state })
      });
    }

    if (reqId !== lastRequestId) return; // stale response
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error("HTTP " + res.status);

    const data = await res.json();
    const prompt = (data && typeof data.prompt === "string") ? data.prompt : "";
    const js = (data && data.json !== undefined) ? data.json : null;

    if (outBox) {
      outBox.textContent = prompt || "No prompt returned by server.";
      outBox.classList.toggle("empty", !prompt);
    }

    if (jsonBox) {
      try { jsonBox.textContent = JSON.stringify(js, null, 2); }
      catch { jsonBox.textContent = String(js); }
    }

    if ($("charCount")) $("charCount").textContent = String(prompt.length);
    if ($("wordCount")) $("wordCount").textContent = String(wordCount(prompt));
    if ($("paramCount")) $("paramCount").textContent = String(countParams(state));

    if (Array.isArray(data.warnings) && data.warnings.length) {
      notify(data.warnings[0], "warn");
    }
  } catch (err) {
    if (reqId !== lastRequestId) return;
    if (outBox) outBox.textContent = "Server error: " + (err && err.message ? err.message : String(err));
    if (jsonBox) jsonBox.textContent = "{\n  \"error\": " + JSON.stringify((err && err.message) ? err.message : String(err)) + "\n}";
    notify("–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–µ", "error");
  }
}

/* Section collapse */
function bindSectionToggles() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".section .section-header").forEach(h => {
    if (h.dataset.clickBound) return;
    h.dataset.clickBound = "true";
    h.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const sec = h.closest(".section");
      if (sec) sec.classList.toggle("collapsed");
    });
  });
}

/* Copy helpers */
async function copyText(id) {
  const el = $(id);
  if (!el) return;
  const t = el.textContent || "";
  try {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(t);
    notify("–°–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ", "ok");
  } catch {
    // fallback
    const ta = document.createElement("textarea");
    ta.value = t;
    document.body.appendChild(ta);
    ta.select();
    document.execCommand("copy");
    ta.remove();
    notify("–°–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ", "ok");
  }
}


async function postJson(url, payload) {
  const r = await fetch(url, { method:"POST", headers:{ "Content-Type":"application/json" }, body: JSON.stringify(payload) });
  if (!r.ok) throw new Error("HTTP " + r.status);
  return await r.json();
}

function resetAll() {
  // clear state primitives
  Object.keys(state).forEach(k => {
    if (Array.isArray(state[k])) state[k] = [];
    else if (typeof state[k] === "object" && state[k] && ("primary" in state[k] || "accent" in state[k])) state[k] = { primary:"", accent:"" };
    else if (typeof state[k] === "boolean") state[k] = false;
    else if (typeof state[k] === "number") state[k] = 0;
    else state[k] = "";
  });
  state.promptFormat = "flat";
  state.referenceWeight = 50;

  referenceFiles = [];

  // clear inputs
  ["mainSubject","textContent","negativePrompt","seedInput"].forEach(id => { const el=$(id); if (el) el.value=""; });
  ["generateFourMode","grid3x3Mode","maxConsistency","beforeAfter","seamlessPattern","skinRenderBoost","hairRenderBoost"].forEach(id => { const el=$(id); if (el) el.checked=false; });
  const img = $("referenceImages"); if (img) img.value = "";
  const w = $("referenceWeightSlider"); if (w) w.value = "50";

  // clear option button actives
  document.querySelectorAll(".option-btn.active").forEach(b => b.classList.remove("active"));
  document.querySelectorAll(".slot-tag").forEach(t => t.remove());

  const outBox = $("promptOutput"); if (outBox) { outBox.textContent = ""; outBox.classList.add("empty"); }
  const jsonBox = $("jsonOutput"); if (jsonBox) { jsonBox.textContent = "{}"; }

  const container = $("imagePreviewContainer");
  const grid = $("imagePreview");
  if (container && grid) { grid.innerHTML=""; container.style.display="none"; }

  scheduleGenerate();
}

async function compactViaServer() {
  const outBox = $("promptOutput");
  const prompt = outBox ? (outBox.textContent || "") : "";
  if (!prompt.trim()) return;
  try {
    const data = await postJson("/api/compact", { prompt });
    if (data && typeof data.prompt === "string" && outBox) {
      outBox.textContent = data.prompt;
      if ($("charCount")) $("charCount").textContent = String(data.prompt.length);
      if ($("wordCount")) $("wordCount").textContent = String(wordCount(data.prompt));
      notify("–û–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ", "ok");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    notify("Compact API –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω", "warn");
  }
}

function downloadText(filename, text) {
  const blob = new Blob([text], { type: "text/plain;charset=utf-8" });
  const a = document.createElement("a");
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  setTimeout(() => { URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href); a.remove(); }, 0);
}

async function translateSubject() {
  try {
    syncTextAndFlags();
    const data = await postJson("/api/translate", { text: state.mainSubject, to: "en" });
    if (data && typeof data.text === "string" && $("mainSubject")) {
      $("mainSubject").value = data.text;
      scheduleGenerate();
    }
  } catch {
    notify("Translate API –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω", "warn");
  }
}

async function enhanceSubject() {
  try {
    syncTextAndFlags();
    const data = await postJson("/api/enhance", { text: state.mainSubject });
    if (data && typeof data.text === "string" && $("mainSubject")) {
      $("mainSubject").value = data.text;
      scheduleGenerate();
    }
  } catch {
    notify("Enhance API –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω", "warn");
  }
}

async function sendToN8n() {
  try {
    const prompt = ($("promptOutput") && $("promptOutput").textContent) ? $("promptOutput").textContent : "";
    const js = ($("jsonOutput") && $("jsonOutput").textContent) ? $("jsonOutput").textContent : "{}";
    await postJson("/api/n8n", { prompt, json: js });
    notify("–û—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ", "ok");
  } catch {
    notify("n8n API –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–µ–Ω", "warn");
  }
}

function setPromptFormatAction(format) {
  const fmt = format || "flat";
  state.promptFormat = fmt;
  document.querySelectorAll(".format-tab").forEach((tab) => {
    const isActive = tab.dataset.actionId === `format-${fmt}`;
    tab.classList.toggle("active", isActive);
  });
  const labels = {
    flat: "Flat (–ü–ª–æ—Å–∫–∏–π)",
    structured: "Structured (–°—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–Ω—ã–π)",
    midjourney: "Midjourney —Å–∏–Ω—Ç–∞–∫—Å–∏—Å"
  };
  const label = $("promptFormatLabel");
  if (label) label.textContent = labels[fmt] || fmt;
  scheduleGenerate();
}

function savePromptFiles() {
  const prompt = ($("promptOutput") && $("promptOutput").textContent) ? $("promptOutput").textContent : "";
  const js = ($("jsonOutput") && $("jsonOutput").textContent) ? $("jsonOutput").textContent : "{}";
  downloadText("prompt.txt", prompt);
  downloadText("prompt.json", js);
  notify("–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–æ", "ok");
}

function randomizeSeed() {
  const seed = Math.floor(Math.random() * 4294967295);
  const el = $("seedInput");
  if (el) el.value = String(seed);
  scheduleGenerate();
}

function clearSeed() {
  const el = $("seedInput");
  if (el) el.value = "";
  scheduleGenerate();
}

window.uiActionHandlers = {
  resetAll,
  translateSubject,
  enhanceSubject,
  setPromptFormatAction,
  sendToN8n,
  copyPromptOutput: () => copyText("promptOutput"),
  compactViaServer,
  savePromptFiles,
  randomizeSeed,
  clearSeed
};

function bindCoreEvents() {
  document.addEventListener("click", handleOptionClick);

  ["mainSubject", "textContent", "negativePrompt", "seedInput"].forEach(id => {
    const el = $(id);
    if (el) el.addEventListener("input", scheduleGenerate);
  });

  ["generateFourMode","grid3x3Mode","maxConsistency","beforeAfter","seamlessPattern","skinRenderBoost","hairRenderBoost"].forEach(id => {
    const el = $(id);
    if (el) el.addEventListener("change", scheduleGenerate);
  });

  const img = $("referenceImages");
  if (img) img.addEventListener("change", handleImageUpload);

  const w = $("referenceWeightSlider");
  if (w) w.addEventListener("input", scheduleGenerate);

  const c2 = $("copyJsonBtn");
  if (c2) c2.addEventListener("click", () => copyText("jsonOutput"));

  // Initial sync of primary/accent UI markers (if buttons exist)
  syncPrimaryAccentUI("lightType");
  syncPrimaryAccentUI("timeOfDay");
  // Action buttons are configured from /api/ui/buttons by /js/action-buttons.js
  setPromptFormatAction(state.promptFormat);

}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  bindSectionToggles();
  bindCoreEvents();
  scheduleGenerate();
});
</script>
